< Review>
Decent little exchange on DLI, it has all the uniform items needed for each branch of service and all the basic items one would need to get situated on base. No real grocery items minus alcohol, bread isle, frozen foods and the like. There is a tailor and a sushi restaurant inside the exchange. The clothing section is good for service members on post but for families and more selection stick to the internet or mall.</Review>

Overall, I definitely think there is room for improvement.... will definitely try again.<//Review>

< Text>
The staff was friendly. The food was served in a timely manner.
In coming to this restaurant, maybe I was comparing this one to one I've frequented over the years in North Hollywood a lil too much.
While the food had it similarities, there were also the not so subtle differences.
The huancaina sauce was a lil too eggy, and the green salsa could've been a lil creamier.
The saltado de camaron and saltado de pollo we're good, and the Inca cola was nice and cold.
Nice atmosphere, with soothing music.
My overall experience was just above average, but try it. You may like it.</Text>

< review>
I've been living here for about 3 weeks now. This review is a reflection of my time here thus far.

Pros: Maintenance staff is prompt with service request and extremely friendly. They greet you even as you are walking about the property. The premises is well kept as well as all the public shared spaces (pool, BBQ's, dog park, tennis courts). Convenience of having a washer/dryer in the apt is definitely a plus. leasing office was available for all questions and responded between 1-2 business days during the process of applying.

cons: not seeing the apartment you are signing your lease for. My apartment was NOT move in ready. I have had to submit a plethora of service requests for small things that should have been fixed prior to my moving in. The apartment was NOT updated. The cabinets are extremely old, and have lazy paint jobs. They hinges on all doors and cabinets were painted over with paint and just allows for a tacky look. The interior trim in the apartment is loose and poorly installed. it is also showing cracks in certain places.  The restroom was a mess- the toilet was not secured at all at the time of move in & the drain to the tub was clogged and the tub is not installed properly. They refuse to fix the tub since it is not noticeably broken.  The apartment was not thoroughly cleaned prior to move in either. There was thick layers of dirt between appliances and in corners and crevices of the apartment. I had to do a deep clean on the apartment and the carpet in the bedroom. After steam cleaning the carpet, the water was disturbingly dirty for having been "cleaned" before my move in. All the cabinets in the kitchen are old and have had so many coats of paint they stick to the wood when trying to open them. There are plenty of small details through out this apartment but theses are just the main highlights.

overall, my advice to anyone considering moving in: urge/request to look at the exact apartment you are moving into. Ensure that all the appliances are working and that the apartment itself will be move-in ready.

definitely regret moving in here. i would have rather allocated my money somewhere else.< /review>

Thank you Corona Pointe Resort for making my stay so pleasurable and memorable. This place is worth every penny.<//text>

I am currently a resident here and the property has been under new management since fall of 2013. The 'heated' pool has not been heated for at least 2 years. When I resigned my lease in February of this year I asked about any future plans for new windows/sliding doors (they are REALLY old) and was told those were not a plan they had yet. A month later those started being replaced from street-view inward. I live near the back of the property. I also find it hard to believe a property this size took less than a month to plan and decide on the best bid for a project of that size and cost. They also repainted all the handrails (which wasn't really necessary). The speed bumps get repainted about once a month which causes driving congestion through the property. The maintenance crew park their golf carts anywhere they like and quite often drive them wherever and however they like. I have actually had one continue to drive head-on toward me and I had to move over and drive on the wrong side of the street to avoid a collision. The newest 'upgrade' is to change all the locks on residents doors that require some sort of special key that you yourself cannot duplicate so they are able to charge you a fee for additional keys. They will issue one for free to each person on the lease and that is all. Another resident here presented the office staff with safety upgrades that were actually needed (like bubble mirrors to eliminate blind spots in turns and a ramp for another handicapped resident) and they received a note on their door that stated they would not be allowed to sign another lease. They have to be out by the end of this month. When this resident questioned the office staff's decision they were told that they 'voted' out and that they are 'too big a headache'. The bubble mirrors are great and I actually feel safer with them there. Handicapped residents shouldn't have to fight for ramps. The law is they should be provided. All-in-all, if you are looking for something in this area you should look at Esplanade, Tuscan Townhomes, Paseo, or basically any place but here. The three I listed already have all the upgrades this place is trying to make with out the headache of a non-concerned office staff and management that bites off more than they can chew. <date>1568405880231< /date><Rate>5</Rate>< review>
I really like these townhouse apartment homes. I used to live in a house and have to transition to an apartment. This was the way to go. You can't find good apartment homes ones with a 2 car tandem garage and a large kitchen, spacious rooms. The pool by the leasing office is great. Leasing office ladies are so nice. I don't know why people are upset. They have been nothing but welcoming and accommodating to me since I moved in. Also, there is a nice little dog park to take my dogs. This complex is very pet friendly. Sure, parking is a tight but which apartment isn't? If you have guests, just go to the leasing office to get a permit for them. There are plenty of spots available for guests, they just have to walk a bit further. If they can't find a spot, they can try to find it off of Kiely. The complex is nicely located between Harker School and a Marriott hotel. Across the street is a shopping center with an asian market, some bakeries, restaurants and Starbucks as well as a Burger King. 7-11 is close by. It's close to the freeway and easy to get in and out of the complex while on Saratoga and also back of the complex. I don't mind living here for a while until I buy a home again. If you are looking for a transition from house to apartment, this is it. Also.. families all over the place. It's wonderful. I have 2 small children and I can say, they love it here.< /review>
